Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical _subprocess_factory=None,\n   357→) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n   358→    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n   359→\n   360→    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one Returns task results and a list\n   362→    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n   363→\n   364→    Args:\n   365→        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n   366→        config: Sprint configuration.\n   367→        phase: The Phase being executed.\n   368→        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n   369→        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n   370→            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n   371→\n   372→    Returns:\n   373→        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n   374→        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n   375→    \"\"\"\n   376→    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n   377→    remaining: list[str] = []\n   378→\n   379→    if not tasks:\n   380→        return results, remaining\n   381→\n   382→    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n   383→        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   384→\n   385→        # Budget check: can we launch?\n   386→        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n   387→            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n   388→            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n   389→            for t in tasks[i:]:\n   390→                results.append(\n   391→                    TaskResult(\n   392→                        task=t,\n   393→                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n   394→                        started_at=started_at,\n   395→                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   396→                    )\n   397→                )\n   398→            break\n   399→\n   400→        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n   401→        if ledger is not None:\n   402→            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n   403→\n   404→        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n   405→        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n   406→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n   407→                task, config, phase\n   408→            )\n   409→        else:\n   410→            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n   411→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n   412→                task, config, phase\n   413→            )\n   414→\n   415→        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   416→\n   417→        # Determine task status from exit code\n   418→        if exit_code == 0:\n   419→            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n   420→        elif exit_code == 124:\n   421→            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   422→        else:\n   423→            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   424→\n   425→        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n   426→        if ledger is not None:\n   427→            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n   428→            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n   429→            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n   430→            if actual > pre_allocated:\n   431→                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n   432→            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n   433→                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n   434→\n   435→        results.append(\n   436→            TaskResult(\n   437→                task=task,\n   438→                status=status,\n   439→                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n   440→                exit_code=exit_code,\n   441→                started_at=started_at,\n   442→                finished_at=finished_at,\n   443→                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n   444→            )\n   445→        )\n   446→\n   447→    return results, remaining\n   448→\n   449→\n   450→def _run_task_subprocess(\n   451→    task: TaskEntry,\n   452→    config: SprintConfig,\n   453→    phase,\n   454→) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n   455→    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n   456→\n   457→    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n   458→    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n   459→    \"\"\"\n   460→    # Build a task-specific prompt\n   461→    prompt = (\n   462→        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n   463→        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n   464→        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n   465→    )\n   466→\n   467→    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n   468→    proc.config = config\n   469→    proc.phase = phase\n   470→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n   471→    _Base.__init__(\n   472→        proc,\n   473→        prompt=prompt,\n   474→        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   475→        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   476→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   477→        model=config.model,\n   478→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   479→        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n   480→        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n   481→    )\n   482→    proc.start()\n   483→    proc.wait()\n   484→    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n   485→    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   486→    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n   487→    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n   488→    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n   489→\n   490→\n   491→def execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n   492→    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n   493→\n   494→    For each active phase:\n   495→    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n   496→    2. Start output monitor thread\n   497→    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n   498→    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n   499→    5. Record PhaseResult\n   500→    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n   501→    \"\"\"\n   502→    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n   503→    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n   504→        raise SystemExit(\n   505→            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n   506→            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n   507→        )\n   508→\n   509→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   510→    signal_handler.install()\n   511→\n   512→    setup_debug_logger(config)\n   513→    import logging as _logging\n   514→    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n   515→\n   516→    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n   517→    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n   518→    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n   519→    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n   520→\n   521→    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n   522→    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n   523→\n   524→    tui.start()\n   525→\n   526→    # Startup orphan cleanup: remove stale isolation dirs from crashed previous runs\n   527→    shutil.rmtree(config.results_dir / \".isolation\", ignore_errors=True)\n   528→\n   529→    # Execute all python-mode phases via preflight executor before the main loop.\n   530→    # Removing this single call reverts to all-Claude behavior (R-051 rollback property).\n   531→    # Lazy import breaks the preflight → executor → preflight circular import cycle.\n   532→    from .preflight import execute_preflight_phases  # noqa: PLC0415\n   533→    preflight_results = execute_preflight_phases(config)\n   534→\n   535→    try:\n   536→        for phase in config.active_phases:\n   537→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   538→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   539→                break\n   540→\n   541→            # Python-mode phases were already executed by preflight; skip here.\n   542→            if phase.execution_mode == \"python\":\n   543→                continue\n   544→\n   545→            # Skip-mode phases: record SKIPPED with no subprocess launched.\n   546→            if phase.execution_mode == \"skip\":\n   547→                _now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   548→                skip_result = PhaseResult(\n   549→                    phase=phase,\n   550→                    status=PhaseStatus.SKIPPED,\n   551→                    exit_code=0,\n   552→                    started_at=_now,\n   553→                    finished_at=_now,\n   554→                )\n   555→                sprint_result.phase_results.append(skip_result)\n   556→                logger.write_phase_result(skip_result)\n   557→                continue\n   558→\n   559→            # Per-phase isolation directory: exactly one file (the phase file)\n   560→            isolation_dir = config.results_dir / \".isolation\" / f\"phase-{phase.number}\"\n   561→            isolation_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   562→            shutil.copy2(phase.file, isolation_dir / phase.file.name)\n   563→\n   564→            try:\n   565→                # Reset monitor for this phase\n   566→                output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   567→                monitor.reset(output_path)\n   568→                monitor.start()\n   569→\n   570→                # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n   571→                if config.tmux_session_name:\n   572→                    update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n   573→\n   574→                # Launch claude with isolation env vars (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR → isolation_dir)\n   575→                _phase_env_vars = {\n   576→                    \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(isolation_dir),\n   577→                }\n   578→                proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase, env_vars=_phase_env_vars)\n   579→                proc_manager.start()\n   580→                started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   581→                # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n   582→                deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n   583→                logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n   584→\n   585→                debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n   586→\n   587→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   588→\n   589→                # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n   590→                # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n   591→                _timed_out = False\n   592→                _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n   593→                _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n   594→                while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n   595→                    if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   596→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   597→                        break\n   598→                    if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n   599→                        # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n   600→                        _timed_out = True\n   601→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   602→                        break\n   603→\n   604→                    ms = monitor.state\n   605→                    _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n   606→\n   607→                    debug_log(\n   608→                        _dbg,\n   609→                        \"poll_tick\",\n   610→                        phase=phase.number,\n   611→                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   612→                        poll_result=\"running\",\n   613→                        elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n   614→                        output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n   615→                        growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n   616→                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   617→                        stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n   618→                    )\n   619→\n   620→                    # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n   621→                    if (\n   622→                        config.stall_timeout > 0\n   623→                        and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n   624→                        and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n   625→                        and not _stall_acted\n   626→                    ):\n   627→                        _stall_acted = True\n   628→                        debug_log(\n   629→                            _dbg,\n   630→                            \"watchdog_triggered\",\n   631→                            phase=phase.number,\n   632→                            action=config.stall_action,\n   633→                            stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   634→                            pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   635→                        )\n   636→                        if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n   637→                            import sys\n   638→                            print(\n   639→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n   640→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n   641→                                file=sys.stderr,\n   642→                            )\n   643→                            _timed_out = True\n   644→                            proc_manager.terminate()\n   645→                            break\n   646→                        else:\n   647→                            # warn action: log and continue\n   648→                            import sys\n   649→                            print(\n   650→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n   651→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n   652→                                file=sys.stderr,\n   653→                            )\n   654→\n   655→                    # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n   656→                    if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n   657→                        _stall_acted = False\n   658→\n   659→                    # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n   660→                    # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n   661→                    try:\n   662→                        tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   663→                    except Exception as _tui_exc:\n   664→                        import sys\n   665→                        print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n   666→                    time.sleep(0.5)\n   667→\n   668→                # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n   669→                # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n   670→                raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n   671→                if _timed_out:\n   672→                    exit_code = 124\n   673→                else:\n   674→                    exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n   675→                monitor.stop()\n   676→                finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   677→                _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   678→                debug_log(\n   679→                    _dbg,\n   680→                    \"PHASE_END\",\n   681→                    phase=phase.number,\n   682→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   683→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n   684→                )\n   685→\n   686→                # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n   687→                # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n   688→                # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n   689→                # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n   690→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   691→                    logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n   692→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   693→                    break\n   694→\n   695→                # Determine phase status\n   696→                status = _determine_phase_status(\n   697→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   698→                    result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n   699→                    output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   700→                    config=config,\n   701→                    phase=phase,\n   702→                    started_at=started_at.timestamp(),\n   703→                    error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   704→                )\n   705→\n   706→                # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\n   707→                # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\n   708→                # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\n   709→                _write_executor_result_file(\n   710→                    config=config,\n   711→                    phase=phase,\n   712→                    status=status,\n   713→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   714→                    monitor_state=monitor.state,\n   715→                    started_at=started_at,\n   716→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n   717→                )\n   718→\n   719→                # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n   720→                error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n   721→                error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n   722→\n   723→                phase_result = PhaseResult(\n   724→                    phase=phase,\n   725→                    status=status,\n   726→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   727→                    started_at=started_at,\n   728→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n   729→                    output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n   730→                    error_bytes=error_bytes,\n   731→                    last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n   732→                    files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n   733→                )\n   734→                sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n   735→\n   736→                debug_log(\n   737→                    _dbg,\n   738→                    \"phase_complete\",\n   739→                    phase=phase.number,\n   740→                    status=status.value,\n   741→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   742→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n   743→                )\n   744→\n   745→                # Log and notify\n   746→                logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n   747→                notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n   748→\n   749→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n   750→\n   751→                # Decide: continue or halt?\n   752→                if status.is_failure:\n   753→                    # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n   754→                    try:\n   755→                        collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n   756→                        bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n   757→                        classifier = FailureClassifier()\n   758→                        bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n   759→                        reporter = ReportGenerator()\n   760→                        diag_path = config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n   761→                        reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n   762→                        debug_log(\n   763→                            _dbg,\n   764→                            \"diagnostic_report\",\n   765→                            phase=phase.number,\n   766→                            category=bundle.category.value,\n   767→                            path=str(diag_path),\n   768→                        )\n   769→                    except Exception as _diag_exc:\n   770→                        debug_log(_dbg, \"diagnostic_error\", phase=phase.number, error=str(_diag_exc))\n   771→\n   772→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n   773→                    sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n   774→                    break\n   775→\n   776→            finally:\n   777→                shutil.rmtree(isolation_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n   778→\n   779→        # Merge preflight results with main-loop results in original phase order.\n   780→        # Build a lookup from phase number → PhaseResult, main-loop results win\n   781→        # on conflict (they are the authoritative executor record for claude phases).\n   782→        _merged: dict[int, PhaseResult] = {r.phase.number: r for r in preflight_results}\n   783→        for r in sprint_result.phase_results:\n   784→            _merged[r.phase.number] = r\n   785→        sprint_result.phase_results = [\n   786→            _merged[p.number]\n   787→            for p in config.active_phases\n   788→            if p.number in _merged\n   789→        ]\n   790→\n   791→        # Sprint finished\n   792→        sprint_result.finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   793→        if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS:\n   794→            # Verify all phases actually passed\n   795→            if not all(r.status.is_success for r in sprint_result.phase_results):\n   796→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.ERROR\n   797→\n   798→        tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n   799→        logger.write_summary(sprint_result)\n   800→        notify_sprint_complete(sprint_result)\n   801→\n   802→    finally:\n   803→        # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n   804→        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n   805→        try:\n   806→            monitor.stop()\n   807→        except Exception:\n   808→            pass\n   809→        if proc_manager is not None:\n   810→            try:\n   811→                proc_manager.terminate()\n   812→            except Exception:\n   813→                pass\n   814→        try:\n   815→            tui.stop()\n   816→        except Exception:\n   817→            pass\n   818→        try:\n   819→            signal_handler.uninstall()\n   820→        except Exception:\n   821→            pass\n   822→\n   823→    # Write sentinel exit code file so tmux caller can read the outcome\n   824→    _exitcode = 0 if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS else 1\n   825→    try:\n   826→        (config.release_dir / \".sprint-exitcode\").write_text(str(_exitcode))\n   827→    except OSError:\n   828→        pass  # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n   829→\n   830→    if _exitcode != 0:\n   831→        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n   832→\n   833→\n   834→def _classify_from_result_file(\n   835→    result_file: Path,\n   836→    started_at: float,\n   837→) -> PhaseStatus | None:\n   838→    \"\"\"Classify phase outcome from the agent-written result file.\n   839→\n   840→    Returns a PhaseStatus if the result file exists, is fresh (mtime > started_at),\n   841→    and contains a recognizable EXIT_RECOMMENDATION. Returns None if the file is\n   842→    missing, stale, or unreadable.\n   843→    \"\"\"\n   844→    if not result_file.exists():\n   845→        return None\n   846→    try:\n   847→        mtime = result_file.stat().st_mtime\n   848→    except OSError:\n   849→        return None\n   850→    if started_at > 0 and mtime < started_at:\n   851→        # Stale file from a previous run — do not trust\n   852→        return None\n   853→    try:\n   854→        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n   855→    except OSError:\n   856→        return None\n   857→    upper = content.upper()\n   858→    if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper:\n   859→        return PhaseStatus.HALT\n   860→    if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper:\n   861→        return PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n   862→    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   863→        return PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n   864→    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   865→        return PhaseStatus.HALT\n   866→    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   867→        return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   868→    return None\n   869→\n   870→\n   871→def _check_checkpoint_pass(config: SprintConfig, phase: Phase) -> bool:\n   872→    \"\"\"Return True if the end-of-phase checkpoint file exists with status PASS.\"\"\"\n   873→    checkpoint_path = config.release_dir / \"checkpoints\" / f\"CP-P{phase.number:02d}-END.md\"\n   874→    if not checkpoint_path.exists():\n   875→        return False\n   876→    try:\n   877→        content = checkpoint_path.read_text(errors=\"replace\").upper()\n   878→        return \"STATUS: PASS\" in content or \"**RESULT**: PASS\" in content\n   879→    except OSError:\n   880→        return False\n   881→\n   882→\n   883→def _check_contamination(config: SprintConfig, phase: Phase) -> list[str]:\n   884→    \"\"\"Return list of artifact files containing cross-phase task ID patterns.\"\"\"\n   885→    import re as _re\n   886→\n   887→    contaminated: list[str] = []\n   888→    artifacts_dir = config.release_dir / \"artifacts\"\n   889→    if not artifacts_dir.exists():\n   890→        return contaminated\n   891→    next_phase = phase.number + 1\n   892→    pattern = _re.compile(rf\"T{next_phase:02d}\\.\\d{{2}}\", _re.IGNORECASE)\n   893→    for md_file in artifacts_dir.rglob(\"*.md\"):\n   894→        try:\n   895→            if pass\n   899→    return contaminated\n   900→\n   901→\n   902→def _write_crash_recovery_log(\n   903→    config: SprintConfig,\n   904→    phase: Phase,\n   905→    contaminated: list[str],\n   906→) -> None:\n   907→    \"\"\"Append crash recovery entry to results/crash_recovery_log.md.\"\"\"\n   908→    log_path = config.results_dir / \"crash_recovery_log.md\"\n   909→    entry = (\n   910→        f\"\\n## Phase {phase.number} — PASS_RECOVERED Recovery\\n\"\n   911→        f\"**Timestamp**: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}\\n\"\n   912→        f\"**Checkpoint**: {contaminated}\")\n   915→        + \"\\n\"\n   916→        \"**Action**: Phase reclassified ERROR→PASS_RECOVERED.\\n\"\n   917→    )\n   918→    try:\n   919→        with open(log_path, \"a\") as runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n\n    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n\n    Args:\n        phase_number: The phase \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n\n    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n    \"\"\"\n    if ledger is None:\n        return None\n    if ledger.can_launch():\n        return None\n    return (\n        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n    )\n\n\ndef execute_phase_tasks(\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n    *,\n    _subprocess_factory=None,\n) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n\n    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n\n    Args:\n        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n        config: Sprint configuration.\n        phase: The Phase being executed.\n        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n    remaining: list[str] = []\n\n    if not tasks:\n        return results, remaining\n\n    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Budget check: can we launch?\n        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n            for t in tasks[i:]:\n                results.append(\n                    TaskResult(\n                        task=t,\n                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n                        started_at=started_at,\n                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n                    )\n                )\n            break\n\n        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n        if ledger is not None:\n            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n\n        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n        else:\n            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n\n        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Determine task status from exit code\n        if exit_code == 0:\n            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n        elif exit_code == 124:\n            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        else:\n            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n\n        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n        if ledger is not None:\n            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n            if actual > pre_allocated:\n                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n\n        results.append(\n            TaskResult(\n                task=task,\n                status=status,\n                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return results, remaining\n\n\ndef _run_task_subprocess(\n    task: TaskEntry,\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n\n    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Build a task-specific prompt\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n    proc.config = config\n    proc.phase = phase\n    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n    _Base.__init__(\n        proc,\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n    )\n    proc.start()\n    proc.wait()\n    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n\n\ndef execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n\n    For each active phase:\n    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Record PhaseResult\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n    \"\"\"\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n        raise SystemExit(\n            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n        )\n\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    signal_handler.install()\n\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\n    import logging as _logging\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # \"\"\"Tests for per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 3) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T02.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Task {i}\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T02.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always succeeds with 3 turns consumed.\"\"\"\n        return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _fail_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always fails.\"\"\"\n        return (1, 5, 512)\n\n    def test_per_task_spawns_one_subprocess_per_task(self, tmp_path):\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(3)\n\n        spawn_count = [0]\n\n        def counting_factory(task, config, phase):\n            spawn_count[0] += 1\n            return (0, 2, 100)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, _subprocess_factory=counting_factory\n        )\n        assert spawn_count[0] == 3\n        assert len(results) == 3\n        assert remaining == []\n\n    def []\n\n    def test_per_task_budget_prevents_starvation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"If budget insufficient for next task, HALT with remaining task IDs.\"\"\"\n        config = TurnLedger(initial_budget=8, minimum_allocation=5)\n\n        def consume_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 5, 100)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=consume_factory,\n        )\n        # First task succeeds, next two should be skipped due to budget\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 1\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert allocate → launch → collect → aggregate\n    with budget verification. (D-0012)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 5) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T03.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Integration Task {i}\",\n                description=f\"Test task {i} for integration\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T03.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_five_tasks_mixed_outcomes(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Full loop: 5 tasks with varied outcomes and budget accounting.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: available reflects actual turn consumption\n        # The executor pre-debits minimum_allocation (5) per task, then reconciles.\n        # Net effect on available: initial - sum(actual_turns)\n        actual_turns = [3, 7, 2, 5, 4]\n        net_consumed = sum(actual_turns)  # 21\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed  # = 79\n        # Verify internal accounting is consistent\n        assert ledger.available() == ledger.initial_budget - ledger.consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Each task consumes 8 turns; budget=25, minimum_allocation=5\n        # Task 1: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=8, avail=17\n        # Task 2: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=16, avail=9\n        # Task 3: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=24, avail=1\n        # Task 4: can_launch? avail=1 < min_alloc=5 → SKIP\n        def heavy_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 8, 500)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=25, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=heavy_factory,\n        )\n\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 3\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert remaining == [\"T03.04\", \"T03.05\"]\n\n        # Aggregate reflects skipped tasks\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.tasks_total == 7  # 5 results + 2 remaining\n        assert report.tasks_skipped == 2\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_all_pass_aggregation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"All 5 tasks pass → PASS status and CONTINUE recommendation.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        def pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=pass_factory,\n        )\n\n        assert all(r.status == TaskStatus.PASS for r in results)\n        assert remaining == []\n\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.status == \"PASS\"\n        md = report.to_markdown()\n        assert \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_total: 5\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_passed: 5\" in md\n\n        #  2→\n     3→## Task: T01.03\n     4→\n     5→## Source Location\n     6→\n     7→- File: `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/executor.py`\n     8→- Function: `_determine_phase_status`\n     9→- Definition: *,\n    17→      config: SprintConfig | None = None,\n    18→      phase: Phase | None = None,\n    19→      started_at: float = 0.0,\n    20→      error_file: Path | None = None,\n    21→  ) -> PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT\n    31→```\n    32→\n    33→### Branch 2 — Non-zero exit (line 995–1016)\n    34→```\n    35→exit_code != 0:\n    36→  Path 1 (lines 998–1004): detect_prompt_too_long(output_file, PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n    43→  Path 3 (line 1016): return PhaseStatus.ERROR   ← DEFAULT for non-zero exit\n    44→```\n    45→\n    46→**Negative exit codes (`exit_code < 0`):**\n    47→- Covered by `exit_code != 0` branch (line 995)\n    48→- Falls through Path 1 check (prompt-too-long likely False)\n    49→- Falls through Path 2 check (checkpoint inference, only if config/phase provided)\n    50→- Reaches line 1016: **returns `PhaseStatus.ERROR`** — no exception raised\n    51→\n    52→### Branch 3 — Zero exit, result file exists (lines 1018–1037)\n    53→```\n    54→result_file.exists():\n    55→  upper = content.upper()\n    56→  has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n    57→  has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n    58→\n    59→  if has_halt → return PhaseStatus.HALT          (line 1027)\n    60→  if has_continue → return PhaseStatus.PASS      (line 1029)  ← CONTINUE sentinel\n    61→  if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", ...) → return PhaseStatus.PASS  (line 1031)\n    62→  if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", ...) → return PhaseStatus.HALT  (line 1033)\n    63→  if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", ...) → return PhaseStatus.HALT  (line 1036)\n    64→  → return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL             (line 1037)  ← result file but no signal\n    65→```\n    66→\n    67→### Branch 4 — Zero exit, no result file, output exists (lines 1039–1045)\n    68→```\n    69→output_file.exists() and output_file.stat().st_size > 0:\n    70→  if detect_error_max_turns(output_file):\n    71→    → return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE               (line 1044)\n    72→  → return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT             (line 1045)  ← THE TARGET STATUS\n    73→```\n    74→\n    75→### Branch 5 — Zero exit, no result file, no output (line 1047)\n    76→```\n    77→→ return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n    78→```\n    79→\n    80→---\n    81→\n    82→## PASS_NO_REPORT Code Path (exact)\n    83→\n    84→**`PASS_NO_REPORT` is returned at line 1045.**\n    85→\n    86→**Conditions required:**\n    87→1. `exit_code == 0` (not 124, not nonzero)\n    88→2. `result_file` does NOT exist (or does not pass the `exists()` check)\n    89→3. `output_file` exists AND `output_file.stat().st_size > 0`\n    90→4. `detect_error_max_turns(output_file)` returns `False`\n    91→\n    92→**This is the broken path for the sprint fix:** when a phase completes successfully (exit 0) and produces output but writes no result file, the executor returns Step(\n            id=f\"{gate_result.step_id}_remediation\",\n            prompt=prompt,\n            output_file=output_dir / f\"{gate_result.step_id}_remediation.md\",\n            gate=None,\n            timeout_seconds=self._config.max_turns * 60,\n        )\n\n    def files_changed(self, step_result: StepResult) -> set[Path]:\n        \"\"\"Return file paths modified during step execution.\n\n        Scans the step's output file and working directory for modifications\n        since the step started.\n        \"\"\"\n        changed: set[Path] = set()\n        if step_result.step is not None and step_result.step.output_file.exists():\n            changed.add(step_result.step.output_file)\n        return changed\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# 4-Layer Subprocess Isolation\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n@dataclass\nclass IsolationLayers:\n    \"\"\"Configuration for the 4-layer subprocess isolation.\n\n    Each layer prevents cross-task state leakage:\n    1. scoped_work_dir: Restrict working directory to release dir\n    2. git_boundary: Set GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES to prevent upward traversal\n    3. empty_plugin_dir: Point CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR to an empty tempdir\n    4. restricted_settings: Set CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR to an isolated tempdir\n\n    The ``env_vars`` property returns a dict of environment variable overrides\n    that should be merged into the subprocess environment.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    scoped_work_dir: Path\n    git_boundary: Path\n    plugin_dir: Path\n    settings_dir: Path\n\n    @property\n    def env_vars(self) -> dict[str, str]:\n        \"\"\"Return environment variable overrides for all 4 isolation layers.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(self.scoped_work_dir),\n            \"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\": str(self.git_boundary),\n            \"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\": str(self.plugin_dir),\n            \"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\": str(self.settings_dir),\n        }\n\n    @property\n    def layers_active(self) -> list[str]:\n        \"\"\"Return list of active isolation layer names for verification.\"\"\"\n        active = []\n        if self.scoped_work_dir.exists():\n            active.append(\"scoped_work_dir\")\n        if self.git_boundary.exists():\n            active.append(\"git_boundary\")\n        if self.plugin_dir.exists():\n            active.append(\"empty_plugin_dir\")\n        if self.settings_dir.exists():\n            active.append(\"restricted_settings\")\n        return active\n\n\ndef setup_isolation(config: SprintConfig) -> IsolationLayers:\n    \"\"\"Create 4-layer isolation for subprocess execution.\n\n    Sets up:\n    1. Scoped working directory (the release dir)\n    2. Git boundary (prevents git operations above release dir)\n    3. Empty plugin directory (no plugins loaded)\n    4. Restricted settings directory (minimal settings)\n\n    All directories are created if they don't exist. The caller is\n    responsible for passing ``layers.env_vars`` to the subprocess.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Sprint configuration providing the release directory.\n\n    Returns:\n        IsolationLayers with all 4 layers configured.\n    \"\"\"\n    base = config.results_dir / \".isolation\"\n    base.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    plugin_dir = base / \"plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n\n    settings_dir = base / \"settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n\n    return IsolationLayers(\n        scoped_work_dir=config.release_dir,\n        git_boundary=config.release_dir,\n        plugin_dir=plugin_dir,\n        settings_dir=settings_dir,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Result Aggregation — runner-constructed phase reports\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n@dataclass\nclass AggregatedPhaseReport:\n    \"\"\"Runner-constructed phase report from collected TaskResults.\n\n    This report is built by the runner, not by parsing agent self-reported\n    output, ensuring accurate task outcome tracking even when subprocesses\n    are budget-exhausted.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    phase_number: int\n    tasks_total: int = 0\n    tasks_passed: int = 0\n    tasks_failed: int = 0\n    tasks_incomplete: int = 0\n    tasks_skipped: int = 0\n    tasks_not_attempted: int = 0\n    budget_remaining: int = 0\n    total_turns_consumed: int = 0\n    total_duration_seconds: float = 0.0\n    task_results: list[TaskResult] = field(default_factory=list)\n    remaining_task_ids: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n\n    @property\n    def status(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Overall phase status: PASS, FAIL, or PARTIAL.\"\"\"\n        if self.tasks_total == 0:\n            return \"PASS\"\n        if self.tasks_passed == self.tasks_total:\n            return \"PASS\"\n        if self.tasks_passed == 0:\n            return \"FAIL\"\n        return \"PARTIAL\"\n\n    def to_yaml(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render the report as a YAML string.\n\n        Produces a machine-readable YAML document with standardized fields\n        for downstream tooling and TUI display.\n        \"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n            f\"tasks_incomplete: {self.tasks_incomplete}\",\n            f\"tasks_not_attempted: {self.tasks_not_attempted}\",\n            f\"budget_remaining: {self.budget_remaining}\",\n            f\"total_turns_consumed: {self.total_turns_consumed}\",\n            f\"total_duration_seconds: {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}\",\n            \"tasks:\",\n        ]\n        for tr in self.task_results:\n            lines.append(f\"  - task_id: {tr.task.task_id}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    title: \\\"{tr.task.title}\\\"\")\n            lines.append(f\"    status: {tr.status.value}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    gate_outcome: {tr.gate_outcome.value}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    turns_consumed: {tr.turns_consumed}\")\n            lines.append(f\"    duration_seconds: {tr.duration_seconds:.1f}\")\n        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n            lines.append(\"remaining_tasks:\")\n            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n                lines.append(f\"  - {tid}\")\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n\n    def to_markdown(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render the report as a markdown string with YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            \"---\",\n            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n            \"---\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"# Phase {self.phase_number} — Aggregated Task Report\",\n            \"\",\n            \"| Task ID | Title | Status | Turns | Duration |\",\n            \"|---------|-------|--------|-------|----------|\",\n        ]\n        for tr in self.task_results:\n            dur = f\"{tr.duration_seconds:.1f}s\"\n            lines.append(\n                f\"| {tr.task.task_id} | {tr.task.title} | {tr.status.value} \"\n                f\"| {tr.turns_consumed} | {dur} |\"\n            )\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        lines.append(f\"**Total turns consumed:** {self.total_turns_consumed}\")\n        lines.append(f\"**Total duration:** {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}s\")\n\n        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Remaining Tasks (Budget Exhausted)\")\n            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n                lines.append(f\"- {tid}\")\n\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        if self.status == \"PASS\":\n            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\")\n        else:\n            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n\n\ndef aggregate_task_results(\n    phase_number: int,\n    task_results: list[TaskResult],\n    remaining_task_ids: list[str] | None = None,\n    budget_remaining: int = 0,\n) -> AggregatedPhaseReport:\n    \"\"\"Aggregate individual TaskResults into a runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n\n    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n\n    Args:\n        phase_number: The phase number being aggregated.\n        task_results: List of TaskResult from execute_phase_tasks().\n        remaining_task_ids: Task IDs that were not attempted due to budget.\n\n    Returns:\n        AggregatedPhaseReport with computed counts and status.\n    \"\"\"\n    report = AggregatedPhaseReport(\n        phase_number=phase_number,\n        task_results=task_results,\n        remaining_task_ids=remaining_task_ids or [],\n        budget_remaining=budget_remaining,\n    )\n\n    report.tasks_total = len(task_results) + len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.tasks_passed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS\n    )\n    report.tasks_failed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n    )\n    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n    )\n    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n    )\n    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n    )\n\n    return report\n\n\ndef check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n\n    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n    \"\"\"\n    if ledger is None:\n        return None\n    if ledger.can_launch():\n        return None\n    return (\n        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n    )\n\n\ndef execute_phase_tasks(\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n    *,\n    _subprocess_factory=None,\n) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n\n    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n\n    Args:\n        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n        config: Sprint configuration.\n        phase: The Phase being executed.\n        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n    remaining: list[str] = []\n\n    if not tasks:\n        return results, remaining\n\n    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Budget check: can we launch?\n        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n            for t in tasks[i:]:\n                results.append(\n                    TaskResult(\n                        task=t,\n                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n                        started_at=started_at,\n                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n                    )\n                )\n            break\n\n        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n        if ledger is not None:\n            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n\n        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n        else:\n            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n\n        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Determine task status from exit code\n        if exit_code == 0:\n            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n        elif exit_code == 124:\n            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        else:\n            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n\n        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n        if ledger is not None:\n            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n            if actual > pre_allocated:\n                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n\n        results.append(\n            TaskResult(\n                task=task,\n                status=status,\n                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return results, remaining\n\n\ndef _run_task_subprocess(\n    task: TaskEntry,\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n\n    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Build a task-specific prompt\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n    proc.config = config\n    proc.phase = phase\n    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n    _Base.__init__(\n        proc,\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n    )\n    proc.start()\n    proc.wait()\n    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n\n\ndef execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n\n    For each active phase:\n    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Record PhaseResult\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n    \"\"\"\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n        raise SystemExit(\n            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n        )\n\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    signal_handler.install()\n\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\n    import logging as _logging\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n\n    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n\n    tui.start()\n\n    # Startup orphan cleanup: remove stale isolation dirs from crashed previous runs\n    shutil.rmtree(config.results_dir / \".isolation\", ignore_errors=True)\n\n    # Execute all python-mode phases via preflight executor before the main loop.\n    # Removing this single call reverts to all-Claude behavior (R-051 rollback property).\n    # Lazy import breaks the preflight → executor → preflight circular import cycle.\n    from .preflight import execute_preflight_phases  # noqa: PLC0415\n    preflight_results = execute_preflight_phases(config)\n\n    try:\n        for phase in config.active_phases:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Python-mode phases were already executed by preflight; skip here.\n            if phase.execution_mode == \"python\":\n                continue\n\n            # Skip-mode phases: record SKIPPED with no subprocess launched.\n            if phase.execution_mode == \"skip\":\n                _now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n                skip_result = PhaseResult(\n                    phase=phase,\n                    status=PhaseStatus.SKIPPED,\n                    exit_code=0,\n                    started_at=_now,\n                    finished_at=_now,\n                )\n                sprint_result.phase_results.append(skip_result)\n                logger.write_phase_result(skip_result)\n                continue\n\n            # Per-phase isolation directory: exactly one file (the phase file)\n            isolation_dir = config.results_dir / \".isolation\" / f\"phase-{phase.number}\"\n            isolation_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n            shutil.copy2(phase.file, isolation_dir / phase.file.name)\n\n            try:\n                # Reset monitor for this phase\n                output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n                monitor.reset(output_path)\n                monitor.start()\n\n                # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n                if config.tmux_session_name:\n                    update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n\n                # Launch claude with isolation env vars (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR → isolation_dir)\n                _phase_env_vars = {\n                    \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(isolation_dir),\n                }\n                proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase, env_vars=_phase_env_vars)\n                proc_manager.start()\n                started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n                # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n                deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n                logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n\n                debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n\n                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n\n                # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n                # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n                _timed_out = False\n                _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n                _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n                while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n                    if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n                    if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                        # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n                        _timed_out = True\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n\n                    ms = monitor.state\n                    _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"poll_tick\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                        poll_result=\"running\",\n                        elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n                        output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n                        growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                        stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n                    )\n\n                    # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n                    if (\n                        config.stall_timeout > 0\n                        and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n                        and not _stall_acted\n                    ):\n                        _stall_acted = True\n                        debug_log(\n                            _dbg,\n                            \"watchdog_triggered\",\n                            phase=phase.number,\n                            action=config.stall_action,\n                            stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                            pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                        )\n                        if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                            import sys\n                            print(\n                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n                                file=sys.stderr,\n                            )\n                            _timed_out = True\n                            proc_manager.terminate()\n                            break\n                        else:\n                            # warn action: log and continue\n                            import sys\n                            print(\n                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n                                file=sys.stderr,\n                            )\n\n                    # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n                    if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n                        _stall_acted = False\n\n                    # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n                    # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n                    try:\n                        tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n                    except Exception as _tui_exc:\n                        import sys\n                        print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n                    time.sleep(0.5)\n\n                # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n                # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n                raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n                if _timed_out:\n                    exit_code = 124\n                else:\n                    exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n                monitor.stop()\n                finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n                _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"PHASE_END\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n                )\n\n                # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n                # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n                # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n                # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Determine phase status\n                status = _determine_phase_status(\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n                    output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n                    config=config,\n                    phase=phase,\n                    started_at=started_at.timestamp(),\n                    error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n                )\n\n                # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\n                # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\n                # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\n                _write_executor_result_file(\n                    config=config,\n                    phase=phase,\n                    status=status,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    monitor_state=monitor.state,\n                    started_at=started_at,\n                    finished_at=finished_at,\n                )\n\n                # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n                error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n                error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n\n                phase_result = PhaseResult(\n                    phase=phase,\n                    status=status,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    started_at=started_at,\n                    finished_at=finished_at,\n                    output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n                    error_bytes=error_bytes,\n                    last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n                    files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n                )\n                sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"phase_complete\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    status=status.value,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n                )\n\n                # Log and notify\n                logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n                notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n\n                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n\n                # Decide: continue or halt?\n                if status.is_failure:\n                    # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n                    try:\n                        collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n                        bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n                        classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                        bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                        reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                        diag_path = config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n                        reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n                        debug_log(\n                            _dbg,\n                            \"diagnostic_report\",\n                            phase=phase.number,\n                            category=bundle.category.value,\n                            path=str(diag_path),\n                        )\n                    except Exception as _diag_exc:\n                        debug_log(_dbg, \"diagnostic_error\", phase=phase.number, error=str(_diag_exc))\n\n                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n                    sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n                    break\n\n            finally:\n                shutil.rmtree(isolation_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n\n        # Merge preflight results with main-loop results in original phase order.\n        # Build a lookup from phase number → PhaseResult, main-loop results win\n        # on conflict (they are the authoritative executor record for claude phases).\n        _merged: dict[int, PhaseResult] = {r.phase.number: r for r in preflight_results}\n        for r in sprint_result.phase_results:\n            _merged[r.phase.number] = r\n        sprint_result.phase_results = [\n            _merged[p.number]\n            for p in config.active_phases\n            if p.number in _merged\n        ]\n\n        #
